  //<![CDATA[
    function loadScript(url, callback) {
      var script = document.createElement("script");
      script.type = "text/javascript";
    
      if (script.readyState) {  //Internet Explorer
          script.onreadystatechange = function() {
            if (script.readyState == "loaded" ||
                    script.readyState == "complete") {
              script.onreadystatechange = null;
              callback();
            }
          };
      } else {  //Other browsers
        script.onload = function() {
          callback();
        };
      }
    
      script.src = url;
      document.getElementsByTagName("head")[0].appendChild(script);
    }
    
    function initAppleId() {
      AppleID.auth.init({
        clientId : 'com.goodreads.app', 
        scope : 'name email',
        redirectURI: 'https://www.goodreads.com/apple_users/sign_in_with_apple_web',
        state: 'apple_oauth_state_1c009368-25c5-4610-8ceb-f6cdc536d6c3'
      });
    }

      var APPLE_SIGN_IN_JS_URL =  "https://appleid.cdn-apple.com/appleauth/static/jsapi/appleid/1/en_US/appleid.auth.js"

<span id="freeTextContainer4979576654083979591"><b>Play with fire, pay the price.</b><br/><br/>Leila’s years on the carnie circuit were certainly an education. What she didn’t learn: how to be a vampire, or how to be married to the most famous vampire of them all.   <span id="freeText4979576654083979591" style="display:none"><b>Play with fire, pay the price.</b><br /><br />Leila’s years on the carnie circuit were certainly an education. What she didn’t learn: how to be a vampire, or how to be married to the most famous vampire of them all. Adjusting to both has Leila teetering on a knife edge between passion and peril, and now the real danger is about to begin…<br /><br />Vlad must battle with a centuries-old enemy whose reach stretches across continents and whose strength equals his own. It isn’t like Vlad to feel fear, but he does…for Leila, because his enemy knows she is Vlad’s greatest weakness. As friend and foe alike align against him—and his overprotectiveness drives Leila away—Vlad’s love for his new bride could be the very thing that dooms them both…</span>
  <a data-text-id="4979576654083979591" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

      </div>
</div>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Jessica&#39;s Totally Over The Top Book Obsession" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Jessica&#39;s Totally Over The Top Book Obsession" href="/user/show/28967089-jessica-s-totally-over-the-top-book-obsession">Jessica&#39;s Totally Over The Top Book Obsession</a>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer863305901" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer14276853253121157952"><b>5 Overcoming Together Stars</b><br/><br/><b>*Spoilers *</b><br/><br/>First read Dec 7 2015 Reread Dec 2 2019<br/><br/><b>"You aren’t just my weakness, Leila.” Vlad drew me next to him, one hand sliding along my jaw while the other caressed my back. “You are my destruction, because if I were to lose you, it would finish me.”-Vlad</b><br/><br/><a href='http://s327.photobucket.com/user/jessica_hatfield1/media/96200-Macklemore-this-is-fucking-awe-AvR5_zps0isghrpw.gif.html' target='_blank' rel='nofollow noopener'>
  <img src='https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1449486877ra/17291732.gif' alt=' photo 96200-Macklemore-this-is-fucking-awe-AvR5_zps0isghrpw.gif' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/>
</a><br/><br/><b>“Leila,” Vlad said in a carefully controlled tone when I sat back down. “I’ve seen enough suffering in my time to know that everyone handles it differently. If you want to talk about what happened, I will liste</b></span>
  <span id="freeText14276853253121157952" style="display:none"><b>5 Overcoming Together Stars</b><br><br><b>*Spoilers *</b><br><br>First read Dec 7 2015 Reread Dec 2 2019<br><br><b>"You aren’t just my weakness, Leila.” Vlad drew me next to him, one hand sliding along my jaw while the other caressed my back. “You are my destruction, because if I were to lose you, it would finish me.”-Vlad</b><br><br><a href="http://s327.photobucket.com/user/jessica_hatfield1/media/96200-Macklemore-this-is-fucking-awe-AvR5_zps0isghrpw.gif.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1449486877ra/17291732.gif" alt=" photo 96200-Macklemore-this-is-fucking-awe-AvR5_zps0isghrpw.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br><b>“Leila,” Vlad said in a carefully controlled tone when I sat back down. “I’ve seen enough suffering in my time to know that everyone handles it differently. If you want to talk about what happened, I will listen. If you don’t, I won’t press you. If you need anything, you will have it. Do you understand?”-Vlad</b><br><br>Bound by Flames, the 3rd book in the Night Prince Series, was Vlad-tastic. But Damn this book goes dark!!! Leila is kidnapped when her and Vlad's house is bombed, she is skinned alive, has her arm ripped off, starved , almost raped, Fake raped twice (Maximus tapes his stuff to him and tapes her too, then has to fake rape Leila while being video taped so the vamp that kidnapped Leila thinks she has been raped), and held against her will for more than a week. The tape of her (fake) rape and of her being skinned alive are sent to Vlad along with her skin that they removed, to drive him mad. See DARK!!!!!!!!<br><br><b>“It changes nothing between us,” he breathed against my skin. “I love you, Leila, no matter what he or anyone else did.”-Vlad</b><br><br><a href="http://s327.photobucket.com/user/jessica_hatfield1/media/Bite-Me-damon-and-elena-15368299-454-304_zpslsrd5kol.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1449486877i/17291733.jpg" alt=" photo Bite-Me-damon-and-elena-15368299-454-304_zpslsrd5kol.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br><b>“Perhaps. I will always have enemies, and though I intend to crush them all, I want your word that you will continue to do whatever it takes in order to survive. You can’t let yourself be crippled by guilt, fear, or hesitation ever again. Promise me.”-Vlad</b><br><br>I can't even begin to tell of the depth of emotion this book pulled out of me. Vlad and Leila in this book were amazing. Leila was so brave and strong. She went through so much and yet she was strong enough to worry more about Vlad then herself. She is a fighter. She did what she had to, to survive. She not only did want she had to she kicked some ass! Vlad, OMG if I wasn't already in love with Vlad I would have been after reading this book. Vlad did some major growing in this book. The way he was with Leila after he got her back, the way he supported her and the things that man said, I melted. Vlad is so raw and sexy in this book, he is like a yummy feral beast. Vlad also really lets his vulnerable side show to Leila in this book. His walls came down, and he starts to really treat Leila like a equal instead of trying to lock her safely away. But don't worry he may show a little vulnerability to Leila, but he is still bad-ass, borderline crazy, pole happy Vlad!<br><br><b>“You’re mine,” he breathed against my neck when his lips left mine to travel lower. “Forever. Say it.” “I’m yours,” I swore, the words ragged from passion. “Forever. Now, take me and prove it.”-Vlad and Leila</b><br><br><a href="http://s327.photobucket.com/user/jessica_hatfield1/media/Cover-teaser_zpspbnpqugj.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1449486877i/17291734._SX540_.jpg" alt=" photo Cover-teaser_zpspbnpqugj.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br><b>“Thank you for answering my questions, and now I want to tell you something personal. It’s not nearly as deep or important, but . . . I’m glad you’re the only man I’ve ever slept with. For years, my voltage issues kept me a virgin whether I wanted to be or not, but then I met you and it felt like . . . you were the one I’d been waiting for, even when I didn’t know it.” My voice caught. “Even with all the awful things that happened, if I was thrown back in time, I would still grab that power line because it’s what eventually brought me to you.”-Leila</b><br><br>Maximus really redeemed himself in this book for me. By the end of the last book, I didn't care much for him. In this book he showed his loyalty to Vlad. My heart hurt for the friendship between them that has been damaged so badly. I hope in the next book they can make up, because Vlad doesn't have many true friends and too many people have backstabbed him in the last few books. I love that Cat was able to finally help Vlad for once and I thought it was sweet that Vlad claimed Katie (Cat and Bones's daughter) as one of his people to help protect her, making him uncle Vlad. We also got a little bit of Mencheres in this book too, but no Ian sadly. Leila's Dad drove me crazy. For real he and Justina should start dating they are both terrible parents. <br><br><b>“I treasure the gift of your virginity, but if you’d given it to another I would still love you to the same dangerous degree. You are in my soul, and nothing you did before we met or will do in the future can change that. And to answer the question you’ve never asked me, yes, I do love you more than I loved Clara. If she were alive now, I would still choose you.”-Vlad</b><br><br><a href="http://s327.photobucket.com/user/jessica_hatfield1/media/782291_zpsnzwgzkgl.gif.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1449486877ra/17291735.gif" alt=" photo 782291_zpsnzwgzkgl.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br><b>“Just because you didn’t torture him doesn’t mean you weren’t rough, but I know why you did it.” I threaded my fingers through his hair. “Thank you for trying to protect me.” The barest smile touched his mouth. “I prefer simply killing people who hurt you. Much less complicated that way.” “Then you showed a lot of restraint,” I said, smiling back because I knew that my dad had been in no danger. “And because I haven’t told you this nearly enough, I love you.”-Leila and Vlad</b><br><br>Bound by Flames was action packed, emotional, sweet, and so exciting that I sped my way through it, unable to put it down. Though it has some dark parts, the romantic parts, the strength of Vlad and Leila's relationship balanced it well. There are even some laugh out loud funny moments. The epilogue was just too damn funny. This was a great read and awesome addition to the Night Prince series. I can't flippin' wait until the last book comes out in 2016. Below I leave my favorite moment from this book:<br><br><b> “Aside from Mencheres, you are the truest friend I have ever had.” Vlad’s voice was so thick from emotion, it was almost choked. “And yet I meant what I said. A good man could forget, but I can’t, and so I cannot reward your loyalty with what I promised. You have no place in my line, Maximus, and you never will.” A harsh sigh escaped Maximus and my heart broke as his shoulders began to shake with suppressed sobs. “I didn’t do this for a place back in your line.” Each word was a rasp. “I did it for you.” Vlad kissed him, once on each cheek. Maximus bent his head until their foreheads touched. “You are my friend forever, voivode meu,” Maximus murmured. “Princes don’t have friends, they have subjects,” Vlad said in an equally low voice. “You are no longer my subject, but even though I will not see you again, you will forever be my friend.” He kissed Maximus one more time on the forehead, and then released him. “Go,” he said, the word as ragged as the regret strafing my feelings. Maximus bowed, turned . . . and paused. “I can’t. The floor’s molten rock and you caved in the only way out.” The barest smile twitched Vlad’s lips. “Rather ruins the moment, doesn’t it?” Maximus’s mouth curled faintly as well. “Good thing neither of us is sentimental.”-Vlad and Maximus</b></span>
  <a data-text-id="14276853253121157952" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

<span id="freeTextContainer16422460687311147683"><i> Reread September 2017 </i><br/><br/>I pretty much feel the same way I did when I first read it. It's been two years and I didn't remember anything, so it was a nice refresher before I read the next book.<br/><br/>--------original review below-----------<br/><br/><b> 4 Dracul-A stars! </b><br/><br/><b> <i> “Love cuts deeper than the sharpest blade, cripples more than shattered bones, and leaves scars that can never fade.” </i> </b><br/><br/><a href='http://s177.photobucket.com/user/dawnygirl07/media/boundbyflames.png.html' target='_blank' rel='nofollow noopener'>
  <img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1423724963i/13663464.png' alt=' photo boundbyflames.png' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/>
</a><br/><br/>Yet another fun and action packed novel by Jeaniene Frost! I will say, I had my doubts about this spin-off series, but Ms. Fro</span>
  <span id="freeText16422460687311147683" style="display:none"><i> Reread September 2017 </i><br><br>I pretty much feel the same way I did when I first read it. It's been two years and I didn't remember anything, so it was a nice refresher before I read the next book.<br><br>--------original review below-----------<br><br><b> 4 Dracul-A stars! </b><br><br><b> <i> “Love cuts deeper than the sharpest blade, cripples more than shattered bones, and leaves scars that can never fade.” </i> </b><br><br><a href="http://s177.photobucket.com/user/dawnygirl07/media/boundbyflames.png.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1423724963i/13663464.png" alt=" photo boundbyflames.png" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>Yet another fun and action packed novel by Jeaniene Frost! I will say, I had my doubts about this spin-off series, but Ms. Frost has made me fall in love with Vlad and Leila.<br><br>In this third (yet not final) book in the Night Prince series, Leila and Vlad have discovered the existance of a once thought dead enemy. I would write his name in the review, but it's so damn weird and complicated, I would have to look back into my paperback copy for the spelling and then copy and paste that shit because dude, it's a weird name. Like souvlaki or something.<br><br>Anyways, Leila and Vlad are doing their best to find their enemy before his finds them, but this is easier said than done. I can't say anymore about the plot without giving it away so I'll stop while I'm ahead.<br><br><a href="http://s177.photobucket.com/user/dawnygirl07/media/pagebreak.png.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1421135336i/13327545.png" alt=" photo pagebreak.png" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>Really loved the development of Leila and Vlad's relationship in this one. It was a giant lesson in marriage being a give and take situation, and both Vlad and Leila did their best to support the other's beliefs and actions to some extent. Well, kind of.<br><br><b> <i> “Compromise Lesson One: Pull a dick move, and your dick gets denied. Every woman knew that, and now, so did the vampire sitting next to me.” </i> </b><br><br>I will say, this book was HOT. And by hot, I mean steamy, and the fact that Vlad literally melted stone. Thats 2000+ degrees F!!<br><a href="http://reactiongifs.com/?p=21061" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1423724963ra/13663465.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>I don't think I've said it before, but because I am a giant nerd I'm going to say it now. Did anyone else watch the tv show Angel? You know, the Buffy the Vampire Slayer spinoff? Well there was a character named Gwen who could electrocute people with her skin. Sounds familiar?<br><a href="http://s177.photobucket.com/user/dawnygirl07/media/gwen.png.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1423724963i/13663466.png" alt=" photo gwen.png" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br><b> <i> "You are in my soul, and nothing you did before we met or will do in the future can change that.” </i> </b><br><br>Well there's not much more to say, this is a weird and short review for me. I absolutely enjoyed reading this book, and now I'm kind of pissed that there's a fourth one out there in the universe. Now just got to wait patiently.<br><a href="http://reactiongifs.com/?p=17473" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1391453956ra/8391092.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1494101706i/22685352._SX540_.png" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br>Follow me on ♥ <a href="http://www.facebook.com/rachelreadsravenously" rel="nofollow noopener">Facebook</a> ♥ <a href="http://rachelsreadsravenously.com" rel="nofollow noopener">Blog</a> ♥ <a href="http://instagram.com/rachelreadsravenously" rel="nofollow noopener">Instagram</a> ♥ <a href="https://twitter.com/rayliz89" rel="nofollow noopener">Twitter</a> ♥<br></span>

<div id="review_1199943607" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1199943607" />
    <a title="Kristen" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/5477946-kristen"><img alt="Kristen" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1312922334p2/5477946.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">

        rated it

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer576841553" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer6463713990808162082">...<br/>...<br/>...<br/><br/><b>NOT WHAT I EXPECTED. </b><br/><br/>It was a great read, but for some reason I just felt there were too many damn pages to describe one short event. And, seriously? Again? Another book about the heroine being kidnapped all over again??? I don't know, it just felt wrong and repetitive. I had truly higher expectations for this series. I used to enjoy reading about the main characters so much, but I never felt like the relationship evolved or changed in any significant way. The story was too similar to t</span>
  <span id="freeText6463713990808162082" style="display:none">...<br />...<br />...<br /><br /><b>NOT WHAT I EXPECTED. </b><br /><br />It was a great read, but for some reason I just felt there were too many damn pages to describe one short event. And, seriously? Again? Another book about the heroine being kidnapped all over again??? I don't know, it just felt wrong and repetitive. I had truly higher expectations for this series. I used to enjoy reading about the main characters so much, but I never felt like the relationship evolved or changed in any significant way. The story was too similar to the previous one. I just wished we had a better insight into the relationship.<br /><br />Mostly the "bad guy" didn't work for me. He had no true motive or any reason at all to justify his actions or act the way he did. He was this big ass who did whatever he wanted when he felt like it, just because... The story didn't have enough content. I could go on reading this series without having read this book at all, and I would not be missing anything at all.<br /><br />While I still love reading anything about Vlad and Leila (as I adore them both), this book just didn't work for me. I hope next is better. </span>
  <a data-text-id="6463713990808162082" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer2541708306" class="readable"

<span id="freeTextContainer14266154909148651628"><b>Play with fire, pay the price.</b><br/><br/><b>
  <i>“You aren’t just my weakness, Leila.” Vlad drew me next to him, one hand sliding along my jaw while the other caressed my back. “You are my destruction, because if I were to lose you, it would finish me.” </i>
</b><br/><br/>This is an another awesome instalment with no stop action. Leila will be taken by Vlad's worst enemy.<br/>Can much can she endure? The torturing? The skinning alive? The dismembering? The lack of blood? The rape?<br/><br/>Vlad will get the audiotapes and once more he will see</span>
  <span id="freeText14266154909148651628" style="display:none"><b>Play with fire, pay the price.</b><br /><br /><b>
  <i>“You aren’t just my weakness, Leila.” Vlad drew me next to him, one hand sliding along my jaw while the other caressed my back. “You are my destruction, because if I were to lose you, it would finish me.” </i>
</b><br /><br />This is an another awesome instalment with no stop action. Leila will be taken by Vlad's worst enemy.<br />Can much can she endure? The torturing? The skinning alive? The dismembering? The lack of blood? The rape?<br /><br />Vlad will get the audiotapes and once more he will see his best friend betraying him. Everything will be burned down without hesitation. He will almost kill all his people. Nobody is as important as Leila. Nobody! She has managed to be his greatest weakness.<br /><br />Vlad will beg and make deals in order to find her. He will use any possible ally. <br />Leila will try to get some blood and get some of her powers back with any way possible.<br /><br />When Leila is saved, they will both feel guilty. Leila will feel guilty because she feels that she betrayed him, while Vlad will feel guilty because he made her a target. <br />But true love is always present. And maybe Vlad and Leila need to be married again to prove it.<br /><br /><b>
  <i>“Love cuts deeper than the sharpest blade, cripples more than shattered bones, and leaves scars that can never fade.” </i>
</b><br /><br />Vlad has always been an old-fashioned guy who needs to protect the females. Leila will prove to him that she can be also a weapon, not just a weakness.</span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/7643503-flo?shelf=fantasy">fantasy</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/7643503-flo?shelf=read-in-2015">read-in-2015</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/7643503-flo?shelf=vampire">vampire</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/7643503-flo?shelf=urban-fantasy">urban-fantasy</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/7643503-flo?shelf=paranormal">paranormal</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer807480483" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer7099924105281092542"><b>3.75 it's Vlad what can I say STARS</b><br/><br/><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1423004699i/13575070.png' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>“You aren’t just my weakness, Leila.” Vlad drew me next to him, one hand sliding along my jaw while the other caressed my back. “You are my destruction, because if I were to lose you, it would finish me.”</i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br/><br/>*sigh*<br/><br/>I had high hopes. Really high hopes...and yeah some of them were met, but it wasn't as perfect as I thought it would be. I had a blast reading never the less. So, let's get this party started!<br/><br/><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1418911509i/12944326.png' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/>Actually we are literally starting with a party. Vl</span>
  <span id="freeText7099924105281092542" style="display:none"><b>3.75 it's Vlad what can I say STARS</b><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1423004699i/13575070.png" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>“You aren’t just my weakness, Leila.” Vlad drew me next to him, one hand sliding along my jaw while the other caressed my back. “You are my destruction, because if I were to lose you, it would finish me.”</i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br><br>*sigh*<br><br>I had high hopes. Really high hopes...and yeah some of them were met, but it wasn't as perfect as I thought it would be. I had a blast reading never the less. So, let's get this party started!<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1418911509i/12944326.png" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Actually we are literally starting with a party. Vlad has invited a few hundred guests for a little masquerade ball and Leila is on touching and unearthing secrets duty. Szilagyi is still at large and nothing would make Vlad - that being Vlad Tepesh...or Dracula, but don't say it to his face or you will regret it...unless you are Bones - so, nothing would make him happier than seeing his arch enemy impaled on his front lawn. <br><br>For those of you new to the party...here is a the backstory in a nutshell...<br><br><a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[Leila had an accident when she was a young girl. In the aftermath she is not only scared, but can also channel electricity and learn a person's darkest sins by touching them. That in return makes her unable to touch people without electrocuting them. <br><br>Until she meets Vlad. He can wield fire and as a vampire he is practically immune against electricity. With his help she learns more about her powers how to deal with them and yeah they fall in love. Throw in enemies who create problems. People die. Leila gets kidnapped a few times and two books later....they are married and she is a vampire after being killed by one of his enemies. Yes, it's all about power and revenge and everyone is very angry all the time. <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span><br><br>Anyway...Szilagyi is Vlad's biggest enemy and he must be stopped at any cost. That's also the agenda for this book in a nutshell.<br><br>Unfortunately said big bad is always ten steps ahead and causes not only immense loss and destruction he has also the power to strike the night prince where it hurts the most...Leila, his wife.<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1418911509i/12944326.png" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1422975955ra/13570866.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>“Vlad loved the same way that he lived--untamable, dangerous, and full throttle.”</i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br><br>Vlad is THE MAN! He is brutal and bloody and he would do just about anything to safe Leila, even sacrificing his whole line. I just love how <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/author/show/669810.Jeaniene_Frost" title="Jeaniene Frost" rel="nofollow noopener">Jeaniene Frost</a> took the original character and made him so much more. Unfortunately I still have the problem that I like him even more when he appears in the Huntress Series. Nothing beats Vlad getting on Bones' nerves and playing BFF with Cat. Hands down. Don't need a love story when I get that particular interaction.<br><br><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>“Our pasts might shape us, but they weren’t the end sum of us”</i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br><br>Leila is a kick-ass heroin who has to deal with a lot of shit this time around, but she takes it like a boss. That woman is strong and just right for dear old Dracula. ;P<br><br>I really enjoyed their relationship a lot more this time around. They felt a lot more like equals and Leila got a break from his overbearing assholishness. In fact both characters seem to be much more on the communicating side in the third instalment. Well, after him trying to make decisions for her leads to more drama than when they listen to each other. And it is much appreciated, tbh. <br><br>I'm not here for Leila being abducted...AGAIN! I'm just done with that story line. I'm sure that are other ways to cause trouble in Vlad's life. Why do they always go for his women. It's boring and the things she has to endure are over the top. Seriously! <br><br><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>“You’re mine,” he breathed against my neck when his lips left mine to travel lower. “Forever. Say it.” “I’m yours,” I swore, the words ragged from passion. “Forever. Now, take me and prove it.”</i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br><br>The hunt for the big bad was interesting and the conclusion has an interesting twist I didn't see coming. But then again it was more of a tool to keep the story going. Did you know that there will be another book? I really thought it would only be a trilogy. Oh well, I guess there was more money to be made.<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1423002112ra/13574720.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>The thing with Jeaniene Frost books for me is that I just love them. I love the world I love how she brings back the characters from the whole <a href="" rel="nofollow noopener">Nighthuntress Universe</a>. The interactions are always golden and make my heart get all nostalgic. I think <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/1421990.Halfway_to_the_Grave" rel="nofollow noopener">Halfway to the Grave</a> was one of the very first PNR books I ever read. So, no matter what, I will pick up her books.<br><br>Here is to hoping that #4 in the <a href="" rel="nofollow noopener">Night Prince</a> series will be fabulous. ;D Now that those two crazy kids actually work with each other. I predict a bright and possibly bloody future ahead and Vlad and Leila sure deserve some happy times. <br><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1418911509i/12944326.png" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><a href="http://coffeeaddictbooks.blogspot.co.at/" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1431601625i/14852808.png" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><a href="https://www.facebook.com/coffeeaddictbooks?ref=tn_tnmn" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1431598100i/14852514.png" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a> <a href="https://twitter.com/flo_reads" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1431598236i/14852521.png" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a> <a href="http://coffeeaddictbooks.blogspot.com/" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1431598236i/14852522.png" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a> <a href="https://plus.google.com/u/0/101016591301224002138" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1431598236i/14852523.png" class="gr-hostedUserImg">

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer483490360" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer7154216165651775806">5/28/16<br/>Need a Vlad fix.....time for a reread.<br/><br/><br/><a href='http://s1186.photobucket.com/user/dshewey1/media/Book%20Review%20Photos/11575720_zpsb424590b.jpg.html' target='_blank' rel='nofollow noopener'>
  <img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1417728809i/12513177.jpg' alt=' photo 11575720_zpsb424590b.jpg' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/>
</a><br/><br/><br/><b>
  <i>5 Fantastic Burning Stars!!!!</i>
</b><br/><br/>WOW!! I <i>looooooved</i> this book!!! Vlad and Leila are back and determined to find Szilagyi no matter what it takes! Well….except Vlad would rather have Leila safely locked away, while he deals with this deadly adversary. However; Leila is very strong willed and is not easily persuaded. She's determined to help her husband with his enemy and It’s not long before Leila lands into evil Szilagyi's hands. His treatment of </span>
  <span id="freeText7154216165651775806" style="display:none">5/28/16<br>Need a Vlad fix.....time for a reread.<br><br><br><a href="http://s1186.photobucket.com/user/dshewey1/media/Book%20Review%20Photos/11575720_zpsb424590b.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1417728809i/12513177.jpg" alt=" photo 11575720_zpsb424590b.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br><br><b>
  <i>5 Fantastic Burning Stars!!!!</i>
</b><br><br>WOW!! I <i>looooooved</i> this book!!! Vlad and Leila are back and determined to find Szilagyi no matter what it takes! Well….except Vlad would rather have Leila safely locked away, while he deals with this deadly adversary. However; Leila is very strong willed and is not easily persuaded. She's determined to help her husband with his enemy and It’s not long before Leila lands into evil Szilagyi's hands. His treatment of her was so horrific, I'm still reeling from it!!<br><br>Vlad is just as brutal as always especially when it comes to protecting his people and even more brutal when Leila’s in danger! Vlad is ruthless in his over protectiveness towards Leila. Where Leila is concerned, there is no one and nothing that will be safe from his savage vengeance (I’m having good shivers right now thinking about it!) <i>I love it when he’s ruthless to his enemies</i>!!!!<br><br><b>
  <i>
    <blockquote>"You aren't just my weakness, Leila...you are my destruction, because if I were to lose you, it would finish me."</blockquote>
  </i>
</b> <br><br>Leila really has come into her own; her electrical power is stronger than ever, she has become a strong heroine although, she still second guesses herself a bit too much. She is young in human years and new to her vampire life (love when Marty calls her <i>“Baby Vamp”</i>). She still can't believe Vlad actually loves <b>
  <i>her</i>
</b> as the storyline progresses, so does Leila's inner strength and she overcomes most of her misgivings when it comes Vlad.<br><br><b>
  <i>
    <blockquote>"Vlad loved the same way that he lived--untamable, dangerous, and full throttle."</blockquote>
  </i>
</b><br><br><a href="http://s1186.photobucket.com/user/dshewey1/media/Book%20Review%20Photos/PicsArt_1464502951507_zpszhtsr6e4.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1464503163i/19245029.jpg" alt=" photo PicsArt_1464502951507_zpszhtsr6e4.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>We get more of Leila’s sister Gretchen who tends to make everyone around her crazy, especially the vampires. I absolutely looooove her character, I’m anxious to see if she hooks up with a Vampire….and maybe becomes one herself?. Her father is still distant and it’s <b>
  <i>really, really</i>
</b> pissing Vlad off!! We’ll just have to see if he gets through to him. <br><br><b>
  <i>
    <blockquote>“You're unnerved by me, so you wish I'd leave the two of you alone to talk?" Vlad snorted. "Your personal discomfort means nothing to me, Hugh ... wait, that's not true. I enjoy it.”</blockquote>
  </i>
</b> <br><br><br><br><b>
  <i>
    <u>WARNING:</u>
  </i>
</b><br>Cat and Bones make a cameo when Vlad needs a little help from his allies, and if you've not read <b>
  <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/10357792.Up_from_the_Grave__Night_Huntress___7_" title="Up from the Grave (Night Huntress, #7) by Jeaniene Frost" rel="nofollow noopener">Up From the Grave</a>
</b>, (which I know a couple of friends here who are stubbornly holding out, not wanting the NH series to end) you will absolutely want to read <b>
  <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/10357792.Up_from_the_Grave__Night_Huntress___7_" title="Up from the Grave (Night Huntress, #7) by Jeaniene Frost" rel="nofollow noopener">Up From the Grave</a>
</b> <b>
  <i>BEFORE</i>
</b> reading <b>
  <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/16173427.Bound_by_Flames__Night_Prince___3_" title="Bound by Flames (Night Prince, #3) by Jeaniene Frost" rel="nofollow noopener">Bound by Flames</a>
</b>, if not you'll get a major spoiler!!! Cat and Bones are not the only characters that show up, we’re also are treated to more Mencheres and Marie aka Ghoul Queen of New Orleans.<br><br><a href="http://s1186.photobucket.com/user/dshewey1/media/Book%20Review%20Photos/flames_zpsbmewriol.gif.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1422545346ra/13513456.gif" alt=" photo flames_zpsbmewriol.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><a href="http://s1186.photobucket.com/user/dshewey1/media/Book%20Review%20Photos/PicsArt_1422499617890_zpshzt7byui.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1422499752i/13506508.jpg" alt=" photo PicsArt_1422499617890_zpshzt7byui.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><a href="http://s1186.photobucket.com/user/dshewey1/media/Book%20Review%20Photos/flames_zpsbmewriol.gif.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1422545346ra/13513456.gif" alt=" photo flames_zpsbmewriol.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>*Once again the extremely talented <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/author/show/2743336.Tavia_Gilbert" title="Tavia Gilbert" rel="nofollow noopener">Tavia Gilbert</a> narrated this audio book!! She is <i>
  <b>FANTASTIC</b>
</i>!!!!<br><br>*Originally read January 2015</span>

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/1113032-uniquelymoi-blithelybookish?shelf=own-have-read">own-have-read</a>,

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1318931711" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer8397501780099188306"> <br/><i>
  <b>5 'I haven't been this excited about a series in ages' stars!!!</b>
</i><br/><br/><i>Bound by Flames</i>, the 3rd book in the<i> Night Prince</i> series is, in my opinion, the best of the 3 so far. It's loaded with twists and turns and things I didn't see coming, things that had me on the edge of my seat, frantic to find out how Vlad and Leila would get out of their current mess - and who was going to die a painful death for putting them in that mess. Vlad takes vengeance to a whole new level, all the while being amazingly</span>
  <span id="freeText8397501780099188306" style="display:none"> <br /><i>
  <b>5 'I haven't been this excited about a series in ages' stars!!!</b>
</i><br /><br /><i>Bound by Flames</i>, the 3rd book in the<i> Night Prince</i> series is, in my opinion, the best of the 3 so far. It's loaded with twists and turns and things I didn't see coming, things that had me on the edge of my seat, frantic to find out how Vlad and Leila would get out of their current mess - and who was going to die a painful death for putting them in that mess. Vlad takes vengeance to a whole new level, all the while being amazingly loving and compassionate in an endearing 'don't make me set your ass on fire' way. :D<br /><br />Once again Tavia Gilbert blew me away with her narration. That woman has talent! The way she seamlessly switches between characters, staying true to their heavy accents and personalities is nothing short of brilliant!<br /><br />Sexy, passionate, romantic, brutally violent, funny... this story has it all and I'm not sure how I'll manage to stay sane while waiting for book 4!<br /><br />Thanks for the buddy read, Bean!<br /></span>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Robin (Bridge Four)" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Robin (Bridge Four)" href="/user/show/14105531-robin-bridge-four">Robin (Bridge Four)</a>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was ok"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was ok</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/14105531-robin-bridge-four?shelf=super-sidekicks">super-sidekicks</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/14105531-robin-bridge-four?shelf=uf-pnr">uf-pnr</a>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer679213238" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer17146870239424764087"><b>Re-read with the girls at BB&B</b>. Still a 2.5 star read for me for the reasons listed below.<br/><br/>Original review Aug 2015:<br/><br/><b>I really wish that Vlad and Leila’s series only took up one book instead of the three.</b> I loved Vlad in the original Night Huntress series but his own stories seemed to have lacked something. He doesn’t play off Leila as well as some of the other characters in the series and that made this side series my least favorite.<br/><br/>Part of the problem is that I don’t really like Leila very much. </span>
  <span id="freeText17146870239424764087" style="display:none"><b>Re-read with the girls at BB&amp;B</b>. Still a 2.5 star read for me for the reasons listed below.<br /><br />Original review Aug 2015:<br /><br /><b>I really wish that Vlad and Leila’s series only took up one book instead of the three.</b> I loved Vlad in the original Night Huntress series but his own stories seemed to have lacked something. He doesn’t play off Leila as well as some of the other characters in the series and that made this side series my least favorite.<br /><br />Part of the problem is that I don’t really like Leila very much. She is so unsure of herself and insecure in a lot of ways. It makes her a little difficult to relate to. In this installment something horrific happens to her and she completely frets over how Vlad might respond to it that she over angst something that ends up being a complete fizzle.<br /><br />This installment of the series probably has the most compelling story line of the three with appearances by Mencharies, Cat, Bones and Marie Laveau as well as former Vlad bff Maximus but there were a few brutal things that happened that were actually a bit too much for me. I’m not a big fan of using rape or threat of rape to build tension and there were chapters where this was the case making my enjoyment of the story a little less. While I appreciate how that whole thing resolved itself Leila’s entire abduction made me a little queasy.<br /><br />If you’ve already read the other two books in Vlad’s series then you might as well finish it out. If you haven’t started Vlad’s spin off yet then it is just okay I’d probably just do a reread of the Night Huntress series instead. <br /><br /><b>Best Book moment was at the end with Vlad’s true confession to Leila about the Dracula myths.</b> I laughed for a good bit over that. The worst book moment involved duct tape and a video camera.</span>

<div id="review_1181410228" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1181410228" />
    <a title="Ferdy" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/4596358-ferdy"><img alt="Ferdy" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1487898103p2/4596358.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1181410228?book_show_action=true">Jan 26, 2015</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Ferdy" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Ferdy" href="/user/show/4596358-ferdy">Ferdy</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was ok"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was ok</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/4596358-ferdy?shelf=blah-romance">blah-romance</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/4596358-ferdy?shelf=boring">boring</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/4596358-ferdy?shelf=evul-people-are-evul">evul-people-are-evul</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/4596358-ferdy?shelf=shitty-parents">shitty-parents</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/4596358-ferdy?shelf=cheesy">cheesy</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/4596358-ferdy?shelf=cringey-romance">cringey-romance</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/4596358-ferdy?shelf=decent-secondary-characters">decent-secondary-characters</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/4596358-ferdy?shelf=urban-fantasy">urban-fantasy</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/4596358-ferdy?shelf=die-heroine-die">die-heroine-die</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/4596358-ferdy?shelf=insufferable-mary-sue-heroine">insufferable-mary-sue-heroine</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1181410228" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer17833993740939996660"><b>Spoilers</b><br/><br/>I really wanted to like this instalment after being disappointed with the first two books in the <i>Night Prince</i> series. I tried really hard not to get irritated by the awful heroine but that failed spectacularly, which was a shame since I actually like the <i>Night Huntress</i> world and have enjoyed past heroines/heroes. I just couldn't with the ridiculous Leila though, she was such a bland insufferable cow.<br/><br/>-There wasn't much of a story, there were no decent twists or turns or good action scenes</span>
  <span id="freeText17833993740939996660" style="display:none"><b>Spoilers</b><br /><br />I really wanted to like this instalment after being disappointed with the first two books in the <i>Night Prince</i> series. I tried really hard not to get irritated by the awful heroine but that failed spectacularly, which was a shame since I actually like the <i>Night Huntress</i> world and have enjoyed past heroines/heroes. I just couldn't with the ridiculous Leila though, she was such a bland insufferable cow.<br /><br />-There wasn't much of a story, there were no decent twists or turns or good action scenes or funny moments. It was a simple plot consisting of Vlad and his enemy (Szilagyi) trying to kill each another. It wasn't thrilling or edge of the seat stuff, it was so obvious how things would play out. <br />It didn't help that Szilagyi was a cookie cutter villain with generic dialogue/actions and petty reasons behind his war with Vlad. Even when he captured Leila and skinned her alive, there was never a moment where it felt like he was intimidating or a genuine threat, he was just so flat and cartoonish.<br /><br />-Leila and Vlad had very little chemistry, their relationship was so forced and nonsensical. I honestly didn't even get why Vlad could have feelings for Leila, how could he have fallen in love with someone so vanilla and generic? On top of that most of the time his 'love' for Leila didn't come across as passionate or even believable, it was plain unconvincing. I did on the other hand believe Vlad's love for Clara (his dead wife), despite Clara only ever being mentioned a few times their love actually came across as genuine and epic, unlike the tepid 'love' Vlad had for Leila.<br /><br />-It didn't help that Vlad treated Leila more like an errant child than a partner/wife. His attitude towards her wasn't sweet or protective it was cringey, and it only ended up making Leila look like a silly, pouty child that didn't fit into Vlad's world. Ugh, it was embarrassing to read their exchanges sometimes.<br /><br />-I absolutely LOATHED Leila's irritating inner voice, did she think she was in <i>Fifty Shades of Grey</i> or something? Her bitchy, insecure, whiny inner voice was one of the worse aspects of her character.<br />Also, all her lame one liners and cheesy threats against far older and powerful vampires didn't make her seem strong or snarky it just made her seem like a grade A thicko.<br /><br />-Was Leila worrying about Vlad and giving him advice to be strong when she was just about to be tortured and raped supposed to be admirable or brave? If anything it made Leila even more of an insufferable corny Mary Sue.<br /><br />-I rolled my eyes at Leila's ridiculous guilt for kissing Maximus when she was out of her mind, what she did was a natural response after getting blood when she'd been starved, but the silly cow did nothing but berate and hate herself for it. She even felt guilty for wanting it to happen again despite only wanting it so she could be strong and healthy for an escape/fight. Her guilt and shame was dumb and over the top considering the dire circumstances she was in. Ugh, her thoughts and feelings about something that was necessary and couldn't be helped were beyond irritating, she was such a twit. Oh, and then there was her guilt at trying to kill Vlad when she'd been spelled to do so and didn't have any memory or control over it whatsoever. Her martyrish-I'm-always-guilty-over-things-I-have-no-control-over personality was infuriating to read and the absolute opposite of likeable.<br /><br />-Vlad used to be endearing, interesting and entertaining in Cat's books but in his own/Leila's he was mostly blah. There was nothing swoony, funny or memorable about him. Even Maximus and Samir came across as more interesting than him. Maybe, I'm just over the cookie cutter alphas with dark pasts and snowflakey powers.<br /><br />-Leila couldn't stop mentioning that whenever Vlad smiled or spoke in a friendly manner it meant he was at his most dangerous, why did she feel the need to keep banging on about that boring, already established and obvious fact? She also kept going on about his powerful aura, his locked out emotions, his secret pain and his tortured past. I already knew about all those the first 50 times she mentioned them all, I didn't need to be hit over the head with his unoriginal and uninspired personality again and again. I'm pretty sure all the repeated mentions of all things Vlad were done to try and make him seem nuanced, enigmatic and interesting but Leila's thoughts were so superficial, repetitive, and banal that it ended up achieving the exact opposite.<br /><br />-What a prick Leila's dad was, she should have told him to piss off after the way he'd treated her for her years. It was obvious he didn't love her all that much, he was the one that was at fault but he blamed her for everything and made her beg and do all the work in their relationship. I wish Leila had gotten a backbone and just told him to piss off instead of acting all sad and pathetic about him.<br /><br />-Loved Gretchen, she was great. I would have much preferred her to be the heroine than boring Leila.<br /><br />-Loved the brief appearances of Cat/Bones/Mencheres. <br /><br />-What was the point of Mircea and the necromancy spell on him/Leila? It felt like he was only added to be another villain-of-the-week so that the series could be needlessly extended to four books instead of three. Ugh.<br /><br />Overall, not a fun read.. Mainly because of the immature-uninteresting-snowflake heroine who thoroughly ruined the story/the hero/the romance. I hope Ian and the other male secondary characters in the <i>Night Huntress</i> world never get their own story, they'll only end up being ruined as well by ending up with some variation of a boring-insufferable-Mary-Sue-vanilla-twit. Ugh, no thanks.<br /></span>
  <a data-text-id="17833993740939996660" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

              <span id="reviewTextContainer1214299182" class="readable"

<span id="freeTextContainer4178542300845280900"><b>3,5 stars</b><br/><br/>Bound by Flames by Jeaniene Frost is the 3rd book in the Night Prince Series, and continues the story of Vlad Dracul and Leila.<br/><br/>This was pretty dark. Leila is kidnapped, tortured, skinned alive, almost raped by the most evil and sinister and menacing vampire ever...Szilavyi, who is Vlad's enemy and who blows up Vlad's home!!! Most of the story is devoted to the horrible things that happens to Leila and Vlad. There wasn't much romance or sex here!!! <br/><br/>The ending felt a bit rushed and of cou</span>
  <span id="freeText4178542300845280900" style="display:none"><b>3,5 stars</b><br /><br />Bound by Flames by Jeaniene Frost is the 3rd book in the Night Prince Series, and continues the story of Vlad Dracul and Leila.<br /><br />This was pretty dark. Leila is kidnapped, tortured, skinned alive, almost raped by the most evil and sinister and menacing vampire ever...Szilavyi, who is Vlad's enemy and who blows up Vlad's home!!! Most of the story is devoted to the horrible things that happens to Leila and Vlad. There wasn't much romance or sex here!!! <br /><br />The ending felt a bit rushed and of course there's the cliff-hanger we left with, which we now have to wait for the next book to come out.<br /><br />My favourite quotes:<br /><br /><b> “You’re mine,” he breathed against my neck when his lips left mine to travel lower. “Forever. Say it.” “I’m yours,” I swore, the words ragged from passion. “Forever. Now, take me and prove it.” <br /><br />“Because love cuts deeper than the sharpest blade, cripples more than shattered bones, and leaves scars that can never fade.” <br /><br />“I’d blush if I wasn’t undead,” </b></span>

<div id="review_1016334795" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1016334795" />
    <a title="Shelly Strange" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/25393430-shelly-strange"><img alt="Shelly Strange" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1600285315p2/25393430.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1016334795?book_show_action=true">Aug 04, 2014</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Shelly Strange" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Shelly Strange" href="/user/show/25393430-shelly-strange">Shelly Strange</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">

              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/25393430-shelly-strange?shelf=hot-guys-alphas-rawr">hot-guys-alphas-rawr</a>,

              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/25393430-shelly-strange?shelf=everyone-loved-it-but-me">everyone-loved-it-but-me</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/25393430-shelly-strange?shelf=3-stars">3-stars</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/25393430-shelly-strange?shelf=read-2015">read-2015</a>,

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1016334795" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer293587775035063758"><a href='https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/958932680?book_show_action=false&from_review_page=1' rel='nofollow noopener'>Once Burned</a>: ★★★<br/><a href='https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/999552168?book_show_action=false&from_review_page=1' rel='nofollow noopener'>Twice Tempted</a>: ★★<br/><br/><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1422591134i/13522132.jpg' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/><i>
  <b>“Get stuffed, don't you have more publicity stunts to pull?" Bones shot back. "How about chatting with another writer who can smear your name into greater popularity?"<br/><br/>"What, did Anne Rice not return your calls, mate?" Vlad asked scathingly. "Jealousy is such an ugly trait.” </b>
</i> <a href='https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/3570231.At_Grave_s_End__Night_Huntress___3_' title='At Grave's End (Night Huntress, #3) by Jeaniene Frost' rel='nofollow noopener'>At Grave's End</a><br/><br/>Sigh. I miss the Vlad from the Night Huntress books. The one who bantered with Cat and tossed adversarial snarky one-liners at Bones. That Vlad is long gone and has been sin</span>
  <span id="freeText293587775035063758" style="display:none"><a href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/958932680?book_show_action=false&amp;from_review_page=1" rel="nofollow noopener">Once Burned</a>: ★★★<br><a href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/999552168?book_show_action=false&amp;from_review_page=1" rel="nofollow noopener">Twice Tempted</a>: ★★<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1422591134i/13522132.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><i>
  <b>“Get stuffed, don't you have more publicity stunts to pull?" Bones shot back. "How about chatting with another writer who can smear your name into greater popularity?"<br><br>"What, did Anne Rice not return your calls, mate?" Vlad asked scathingly. "Jealousy is such an ugly trait.” </b>
</i> <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/3570231.At_Grave_s_End__Night_Huntress___3_" title="At Grave's End (Night Huntress, #3) by Jeaniene Frost" rel="nofollow noopener">At Grave's End</a><br><br>Sigh. I miss the Vlad from the Night Huntress books. The one who bantered with Cat and tossed adversarial snarky one-liners at Bones. That Vlad is long gone and has been since book one of this series. At least he isn't as annoying in this book as he was in the last one, though.<br><br>Bound by Flames pretty much picks up where <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/13125234.Twice_Tempted__Night_Prince___2_" title="Twice Tempted (Night Prince, #2) by Jeaniene Frost" rel="nofollow noopener">Twice Tempted</a> left off. Vlad and Leila are still struggling in their relationship/marriage and trying to find Vlad's arch-nemesis, Szilagy. There are some good scenes, which is why I am rating this 3 stars. Basically, the highlight was seeing some old favorites from the Night Huntress world (Cat, Bones, Mencheres, even the Queen of the Ghouls shows up, Marie Laveau). I like Marty too. Gretchen (Leila's sister) is mildly entertaining. <br><br>Leila does absolutely nothing for me as a heroine and female protagonist. She's pretty boring and she and Vlad have little chemistry that I can see. Yes, they do seem to be progressing in their relationship and there isn't as much angst that makes you want drive a metal spike into your brain like there was in the previous books. <br><br>The writing is fine. I just don't think this couple has any sparks, although they literally should, with his fire power and her electrical abilities. It just ultimately fell flat for me. I think Maximus comes across as more interesting than Vlad does. (Maximus is Vlad's oldest friend, and is a carryover from the other books, yet there is troubled history between them because of Leila. He kind of redeems himself in this, but is dismissed in the end by Vlad because Vlad is, well frankly, he's pretty much always a d!ck in this series. Whatever.) <br><br>I just can't muster up any feels for these books anymore. But I am so down for a re-read of Night Huntress. BONES. IAN. Yesssssssssssssss please.</span>
  <a data-text-id="293587775035063758" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

<div id="review_618929855" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/618929855" />
    <a title="Eva Rose" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/10336770-eva-rose"><img alt="Eva Rose" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1539733423p2/10336770.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/618929855?book_show_action=true">May 18, 2013</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Eva Rose" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Eva Rose" href="/user/show/10336770-eva-rose">Eva Rose</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="did not like it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">did not like it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/10336770-eva-rose?shelf=sexy-books">sexy-books</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/10336770-eva-rose?shelf=adult-fiction">adult-fiction</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/10336770-eva-rose?shelf=vampires">vampires</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/10336770-eva-rose?shelf=urban-fantasy">urban-fantasy</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/10336770-eva-rose?shelf=guilty-pleasure">guilty-pleasure</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/10336770-eva-rose?shelf=paranormal-romance">paranormal-romance</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/10336770-eva-rose?shelf=january">january</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/10336770-eva-rose?shelf=2015-publication">2015-publication</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/10336770-eva-rose?shelf=girls-with-guns-swords-and-magic">girls-with-guns-swords-and-magic</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer618929855" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer7864602283761813887">This book was a sad clusterfuck. <br/><br/><a href='http://s1191.photobucket.com/user/alice_no_good/media/HCfpo_zpstys6gl4a.gif.html' target='_blank' rel='nofollow noopener'>
  <img src='https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1425171160ra/13856924.gif' alt=' photo HCfpo_zpstys6gl4a.gif' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/>
</a><br/><br/>I am really disappointed with how this book turned out, I was expecting for the plot to <i>at least</i> make some sense. Plus, the ending plot twist felt tack on to continue to write this series to death. Not to mention that Leila getting kidnapped and tortured has become a bit of a tradition in this series. <br/><br/>This ugly trend is only compounded by her rape, Frost wrote it out as her wanting it but Leila was overtaken with bloodlust, and Maximus was NOT, so he raped he</span>
  <span id="freeText7864602283761813887" style="display:none">This book was a sad clusterfuck. <br><br><a href="http://s1191.photobucket.com/user/alice_no_good/media/HCfpo_zpstys6gl4a.gif.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1425171160ra/13856924.gif" alt=" photo HCfpo_zpstys6gl4a.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>I am really disappointed with how this book turned out, I was expecting for the plot to <i>at least</i> make some sense. Plus, the ending plot twist felt tack on to continue to write this series to death. Not to mention that Leila getting kidnapped and tortured has become a bit of a tradition in this series. <br><br>This ugly trend is only compounded by her rape, Frost wrote it out as her wanting it but Leila was overtaken with bloodlust, and Maximus was NOT, so he raped her. The funny thing is that since he was trying to feed her and no one was supposed to know about it, since she was in captivity and he was a double agent, it is all pass off as a noble act of self sacrifice and I just can't stomach it. She was in a hunger frenzy from denied blood for days, pressing against him and acting mindlessly. That doesn't give Maximus a pass to penetrate her, yet he did and it makes me angry. Maximus is supposed to have ironclad control over his impulses, he isn't a teenager.<br><br>After this I don't think I can read another one of Frost works again because not only does she write rape, she passed it off as Maximus not being able to control himself. Plus, her plots are a clusterfuck and I have grown tire of her incompetent prose.</span>
  <a data-text-id="7864602283761813887" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/497185985?book_show_action=true">Jan 05, 2013</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Sharon ∞❥ is an emotional book junkie ❥∞ " class="user" itemprop="url" name="Sharon ∞❥ is an emotional book junkie ❥∞ " href="/user/show/3275325-sharon-is-an-emotional-book-junkie">Sharon ∞❥ is an emotional book junkie ❥∞ </a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>

          <a class="lightGreyText" title="ebook 9780062075826" href="/book/show/22500564-bound-by-flames">review of another edition</a>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer497185985" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer9155026345765971616">Vlad's still the bad@ss, Leila's still asserting herself...and dealing with her "new" self and they're still after the bad guy. Only this time, the "bad guy" is ahead of them.<br/><br/><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1423168653i/13594630._SY540_.png' width='350' height='400' alt='description' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/>One of my issues is that Vlad's "book" has definitely become its own series. I had to keep reminding myself of that and not feel like it was being dragged out! <br/><br/>The one good thing is that there is a lot of progression with Vlad. Granted he is <i>always</i> domineering and doesn't always listen but I felt there were a lot of breakth</span>
  <span id="freeText9155026345765971616" style="display:none">Vlad's still the bad@ss, Leila's still asserting herself...and dealing with her "new" self and they're still after the bad guy. Only this time, the "bad guy" is ahead of them.<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1423168653i/13594630._SY540_.png" width="350" height="400" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>One of my issues is that Vlad's "book" has definitely become its own series. I had to keep reminding myself of that and not feel like it was being dragged out! <br><br>The one good thing is that there is a lot of progression with Vlad. Granted he is <i>always</i> domineering and doesn't always listen but I felt there were a lot of breakthroughs with him and Leila. I was really happy to see that because it's been one of the things that really bothered me in the past books. <br><br>Leila is getting better too. She is trying to listen more and learn from Vlad. I hate what happened to her but thank goodness for Maximus. <br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1423168653ra/13594645.gif" width="400" height="250" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>I just love the intensity between these two. I think by getting in there and working out the kinks, they have come together on a much deeper level. <br><br>Dealing with Szilagyi was frustrating especially when the spells started coming out. It seemed like it was never going to end! The twist at the end was unexpected. <br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1423168653ra/13594631.gif" width="400" height="250" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>And the parts with Maximus and Vlad...that was a killer. I loved seeing those sides of both of them. I definitely would like more! <br><br>Anybody else feeling a Gretchen and Samir pairing? LOL!<br><br>I did like how things ended but I'm really hoping the next book is it and things get wrapped up. I'm still waiting for an Ian book! *fingers crossed*<br><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1423168653i/13594637._SX540_.png" width="400" height="150" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><b>
  <u>Favorite quotes:</u>
</b><br><br>♥ "Compromise Lesson One: Pull a dick move, and your dick gets denied. Every woman knew that, and now, so did the vampire sitting next to me."<br><br>♥ "You aren’t just my weakness, Leila.” Vlad drew me next to him, one hand sliding along my jaw while the other caressed my back. “You are my destruction, because if I were to lose you, it would finish me.”<br><br>♥ "Vlad loved the same way that he lived--untamable, dangerous, and full throttle."<br><br>♥ "You’re the bastard daughter of a diseased whore.” <br><br>I snorted. “Have to give it to you older vamps. Your insults are much more colorful than my generation’s variations on ‘f*ck you, you f*cking f*ck.’”<br><br>♥ “I didn’t do this for a place back in your line.” Each word was a rasp. “I did it for you.”<br></span>

<div id="review_823352679" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/823352679" />

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/823352679?book_show_action=true">Jan 14, 2014</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Mikky (Nocturnal Predators Reviews)" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Mikky (Nocturnal Predators Reviews)" href="/user/show/20583675-mikky-nocturnal-predators-reviews">Mikky (Nocturnal Predators Reviews)</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/20583675-mikky-nocturnal-predators-reviews?shelf=read-in-2020">read-in-2020</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/20583675-mikky-nocturnal-predators-reviews?shelf=read-in-2015">read-in-2015</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer823352679" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer13711771575442946575"><b>Update After Rereading July 2020:</b> It seems like I was very harsh on this series during my first read-through. I had a lasting impression that Vlad was a domineering overpowering a**, but after thinking it through and with the revelations throughout these books so far he's actually not that bad. I must have been projecting my problems on Vlad at the time because I've done a complete 180 on where I stand on these books. Also, my anger with Leila's family this time around is nonexistent. They're th</span>
  <span id="freeText13711771575442946575" style="display:none"><b>Update After Rereading July 2020:</b> It seems like I was very harsh on this series during my first read-through. I had a lasting impression that Vlad was a domineering overpowering a**, but after thinking it through and with the revelations throughout these books so far he's actually not that bad. I must have been projecting my problems on Vlad at the time because I've done a complete 180 on where I stand on these books. Also, my anger with Leila's family this time around is nonexistent. They're there and they serve a very small purpose for Leila's character development and the plot but that's about it. I don't really like or dislike them at this point.<br><br><i>My Updated Rating: 4 Stars </i><br>____________________<br>Originally posted at:<br><a href="http://www.nocturnalpredatorsreviews.blogspot.com" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1389562756i/8040458.png" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br><i>My Rating: 3 Stars</i><br><br>Painfully neutral are the words I'd use to describe my feelings for this book. How unfortunate because I was looking forward to this releasing. I can say one thing: I LOVE that cover.<br><br>Leila is as kick a** as ever. She's actually one of the things I liked about this book. She finds a way to survive torture (for the second time) and defeat the enemy, all the while keeping her boyfriend happy.<br><br>Speaking of Dracula....<i>oh I'm sorry Vlad Dracul</i>. He's gotten too domineering and over baring. Leila had to suffer another (third) round of torture because he was trying to protect her in a mansion everyone knew was his and that she was staying there. There was absolutely NO CHANCE, not even 0.1% that the enemy would attack, right? <b>RIGHT?</b><br><br>Also what does Leila's family do for the plot/storyline? My guess: add drama. Other then a few smart remarks from Gretchen there was barely any character development whatsoever. Which was disappointing because I wanted to see if her father would finally understand what happened as a necessity and accept it as a fact of life.<br><br>Final thoughts: I will probably end up buying the next book (last?) because of the awesome cover I already envision it having, but I'm not sure I care enough about the characters at this point to actually summon up some reaction to the mild cliffhanger.<br><br><b>My Favorite Quotes:</b><br><br><i>"Playing dead worked when confronted with an angry grizzly, but Vlad was more like a dragon. You either fought back or you got your ass burned off while you ran away."<br><br>"The nine pounds Gretchen had gained must've come from her new brass balls."<br><br>"Because love cuts deeper than the sharpest blade, cripples more than shattered bones, and leaves scars that can never fade."</i></span>
  <a data-text-id="13711771575442946575" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>

        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>
