        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer573528804" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer11858204956390347049">4.5 STARS<br/><br/>This is such a fantastic series! Filled with action, mystery and loads of romance, you seriously can't go wrong. I love Vlad, I love his over drawn and explosive intensity. I don't even think intense is a word that does this man justice, but I can't think of another word that fits him so well. I knew he loved Leila, but here he proved it numerous times to the point where the depth of his feelings for her verged on wholly dangerous. But that made me love him even more! <br/>And Leila is one o</span>
  <span id="freeText11858204956390347049" style="display:none">4.5 STARS<br /><br />This is such a fantastic series! Filled with action, mystery and loads of romance, you seriously can't go wrong. I love Vlad, I love his over drawn and explosive intensity. I don't even think intense is a word that does this man justice, but I can't think of another word that fits him so well. I knew he loved Leila, but here he proved it numerous times to the point where the depth of his feelings for her verged on wholly dangerous. But that made me love him even more! <br />And Leila is one of my favorite ever heroines. She's confident yet questions herself all the time. I love that she never tries to be someone else or act any differently because she's now a vampire. She's kind and loving, brave and vulnerable, dangerous yet protective. This time around she had to prove to Vlad that she's better off fighting adversaries with him rather than hiding out. There were some very traumatic scenes with her here solely because of Vlad's overprotectiveness that put her in danger. Yet she persevered and came out stronger. I loved seeing Vlad see the error of his ways and finally give in to helping Leila HELP him. <br />We got a cameo of Kat and Bones and a spoiler along with them...which surprised me, but no biggie cause I'll finish their series soon anyways. There is still one book left in this particular series and with the way this one ends, I know what the sole purpose of that book will be. But regardless, Leila and Vlad are in a beautiful place, a place they had to fight for but it makes it all the more sweeter! Can't wait for the final book!</span>
  <a data-text-id="11858204956390347049" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

<div id="review_572284267" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/572284267" />
    <a title="Carmel (Rabid Reads)" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/4561998-carmel-rabid-reads"><img alt="Carmel (Rabid Reads)" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1396922701p2/4561998.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/572284267?book_show_action=true">Mar 27, 2013</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Carmel (Rabid Reads)" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Carmel (Rabid Reads)" href="/user/show/4561998-carmel-rabid-reads">Carmel (Rabid Reads)</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>

          <span class="greyText">&nbsp;&middot;&nbsp;</span>
          <a class="lightGreyText" title="Audiobook 9780062129451" href="/book/show/16065507-bound-by-flames">review of another edition</a>


        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/4561998-carmel-rabid-reads?shelf=audio">audio</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/4561998-carmel-rabid-reads?shelf=audio-2015">audio-2015</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer572284267" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer10833635532373434696"><b>Reviewed by: <a href='http://rabidreads.ca/2015/02/audiobook-review-bound-by-flames-by-jeaniene-frost.html' rel='nofollow noopener'>Rabid Reads</a></b>.<br/><br/>Jeaniene Frost is renowned the world over for her oh-my-god-is-it-hot-in-here scenes, but she can also rock the dark like nobody’s business, and readers were reminded of that fact with a vengeance in BOUND BY FLAMES. Graphic torture anyone? I’m talking flaying, limb amputation, silver poisoning, starvation, and pseudo rape. This installment was originally intended to be the finale of the NIGHT PRINCE series; however after listening to book 3, I can understand why the aut</span>
  <span id="freeText10833635532373434696" style="display:none"><b>Reviewed by: <a href="http://rabidreads.ca/2015/02/audiobook-review-bound-by-flames-by-jeaniene-frost.html" rel="nofollow noopener">Rabid Reads</a></b>.<br /><br />Jeaniene Frost is renowned the world over for her oh-my-god-is-it-hot-in-here scenes, but she can also rock the dark like nobody’s business, and readers were reminded of that fact with a vengeance in BOUND BY FLAMES. Graphic torture anyone? I’m talking flaying, limb amputation, silver poisoning, starvation, and pseudo rape. This installment was originally intended to be the finale of the NIGHT PRINCE series; however after listening to book 3, I can understand why the author decided to axe that plan. A new super villain has risen, Vlad &amp; Leila didn’t get their HEA, and there’s still plenty of story left to tell!<br /><br />I’ve had a jumbo crush on Tepesh ever since his character debuted as a secondary in Frost’s NIGHT HUNTRESS novels, and it’s steadily grown into an all out obsession with this spin-off series. He could easily be king of the bad guys if it weren’t for Mrs. Dracula which makes him the ultimate antihero. We got to see a more vulnerable side to Vlad in this installment while as Leila was all steel and resolve. The balance of power in their relationship has been markedly one-sided until now, so I loved the role reversal, and as expected, the author didn’t hold back on the ravishing either. *winks*<br /><br />Maximus drove me nutso in the best kind of way, and I was happy that Leila’s father finally saw reason after his prolonged silent treatment of his daughter. Marty was as primo as always, and my hankering for a Cat &amp; Bones cameo was quenched, although it’s worth pointing out that their part was somewhat spoiler-y if you haven’t read UP FROM THE GRAVE yet. Mencheres also popped in to say hi which made my character driven self very jubilant. You’ll notice that I’m glossing over the plot, and that’s because it puts to bed the main story arc, so I’m not willing to risk accidentally spilling the beans, but it’s DA BOMB!<br /><br />This was my first time listening to a NIGHT PRINCE audiobook, however I was already acquainted with Tavia Gilbert as a narrator, so I had zero quibbles about her performance going in. Her renditions of both of the protagonists were on par with those that I had inside my head prior to her voice taking them over. I’m a sucker for accents, and her English (Bones), Romanian (Vlad), and New Orleans (Marie) vernacular left me tickled pink. I’m still trying to determine whether it was the narration or the writing that has me dubbing this as my favourite installment, either way, I loved it!<br /><br />BOUND BY FLAMES will make you break out into a Snoopy happy dance!</span>
  <a data-text-id="10833635532373434696" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

<div id="review_2200420401" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/2200420401" />
    <a title="Cece ❀Rants, Raves &amp;Reviews❀" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/66199133-cece-rants-raves-reviews"><img alt="Cece ❀Rants, Raves &amp;Reviews❀" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1492999740p2/66199133.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/2200420401?book_show_action=true">Nov 30, 2017</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Cece ❀Rants, Raves &amp;Reviews❀" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Cece ❀Rants, Raves &amp;Reviews❀" href="/user/show/66199133-cece-rants-raves-reviews">Cece ❀Rants, Raves &amp;Reviews❀</a>

        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>

            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/66199133-cece-rants-raves-reviews?shelf=erotic-romance">erotic-romance</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/66199133-cece-rants-raves-reviews?shelf=reviews-of-the-year">reviews-of-the-year</a>,

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer2200420401" class="readable"

<span id="freeTextContainer824027851972842898">While the other books in this series had tension and fights, this book... <b>shit went dowh, hella dark, and it broke my godddamn heart</b> damn i’m such a poet <br/><br/><b>Leila</b> is a sweet caring proper young lady who is <b>never reckless</b> and really thinks about the consequences of all her actions<br/><br/><b>
  <i>“Let me go, I need to do this,” I tried to say, but the words came out unintelligible. Unable to talk, I glared at him. Couldn’t he see that I had to cut my head off? Right now?”</i>
</b><br/><br/>Leila’s character isn’t as bloodthirsty a</span>
  <span id="freeText824027851972842898" style="display:none">While the other books in this series had tension and fights, this book... <b>shit went dowh, hella dark, and it broke my godddamn heart</b> damn i’m such a poet <br /><br /><b>Leila</b> is a sweet caring proper young lady who is <b>never reckless</b> and really thinks about the consequences of all her actions<br /><br /><b>
  <i>“Let me go, I need to do this,” I tried to say, but the words came out unintelligible. Unable to talk, I glared at him. Couldn’t he see that I had to cut my head off? Right now?”</i>
</b><br /><br />Leila’s character isn’t as bloodthirsty as Cat but she does her equal share of cussing out vampires before kicking their asses<br /><br /><b>
  <i>“He turned around to glare at me. “Want it in English? Fine. You’re the bastard daughter of a diseased whore.”<br />I snorted. “Have to give it to you older vamps. Your insults are much more colorful than my generation’s variations on ‘fuck you, you fucking fuck.”</i>
</b><br /><br />I loved <u>Leila and Vlad’s dynamic</u>~~ it was hilarious, swooning, and just cliche made for each other<br /><br /><b>
  <i>“Vlad flashed a tolerant look at Mencheres. “Pay this no mind. She always argues with me when I propose to her.”</i>
</b><br /><br />He is the only authentic Vlad. <u>
  <b>All other vampires are just imitations. </b>
</u><br /><br /><b>Vlad</b> is one of the most complex characters i have ever read. <b>He is damaged but dangerous</b>, complex but lives by simple rules... and he is so goddamn sexy. I loved Vlad’s character in the first series so it was awesome getting to learn more about him. <br /><br /><b>
  <i>“Vlad opened his eyes, <u>torment</u> reflecting in his coppery green depths. “I am responsible for the Dracula hype.”<br />I stared at him, certain that I must have briefly gone insane and misheard him. “What”</i>
</b><br /><br />In general, this series is pretty action packed with flares of humor wrapped around the stupidity of the bad guys <br /><br /><b>
  <i> “I couldn’t help it—I laughed with demented amusement. After all the backfiring I’d experienced with my abilities, the necromancer’s spell biting him in the ass in such a stupendous way was the most hilarious thing I’d heard all month.”</i>
</b><br /><br /> But this book went down a darker road with torture and godddamn it the separation and the <b>pain</b> and <b>feels</b> and <b>hurt</b> and <b>shit blowing up</b>. I almost cried like three times, im just saying this is not for the light of heart</span>

  <div class="left bodycol">

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>

            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/3108364-francesca-the-fierce-under-the-covers-book-blog?shelf=genre-paranormal-romance">genre-paranormal-romance</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/3108364-francesca-the-fierce-under-the-covers-book-blog?shelf=i-had-to-read-again">i-had-to-read-again</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/3108364-francesca-the-fierce-under-the-covers-book-blog?shelf=read-audio-books">read-audio-books</a>,

              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/3108364-francesca-the-fierce-under-the-covers-book-blog?shelf=books-read-2015">books-read-2015</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer483403625" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer13891021277674660279"><a href='http://www.underthecoversbookblog.com/2015/01/arc-review-blitz-bound-by-flames-by-jeaniene-frost.html' rel='nofollow noopener'>
  <img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1430489640i/14717740.jpg' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/>
</a><br/><br/>I’m not quite sure where to start. But let me tell you one thing…. Jeaniene Frost still got it! BOUND BY FLAMES blew me away, kept me riveted and kept my adrenaline pumping. This book lives up to every expectation I didn’t even know I had. Yeah, it’s that good. Vlad is back with a vengeance! This is the Vlad I fell in love with in the Night Huntress series. Ruthless, possessive, exasperating, pure dominant alpha male. Did I mention Vlad tended toward the brutal side of archaic? I think there</span>
  <span id="freeText13891021277674660279" style="display:none"><a href="http://www.underthecoversbookblog.com/2015/01/arc-review-blitz-bound-by-flames-by-jeaniene-frost.html" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1430489640i/14717740.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>I’m not quite sure where to start. But let me tell you one thing…. Jeaniene Frost still got it! BOUND BY FLAMES blew me away, kept me riveted and kept my adrenaline pumping. This book lives up to every expectation I didn’t even know I had. Yeah, it’s that good. Vlad is back with a vengeance! This is the Vlad I fell in love with in the Night Huntress series. Ruthless, possessive, exasperating, pure dominant alpha male. Did I mention Vlad tended toward the brutal side of archaic? I think there will be a lot of Vlad gushing in this review, so excuse me from now.<br><br>I don’t want to give too much away from the story. Just know that Vlad is still fighting his number one enemy. And this is a big sneaky one! As far as bad guys go, Ms. Frost gives Vlad a run for his money with this guy. Definitely a worthy opponent and one that really kept me on my toes and kept shocking me! Making this such an action packed story.<br><br>Leila, let’s talk about her. She’s more and more like Cat for me. She’s growing, she’s learning, she’s tough, and she will fight tooth and nail for her love and her relationship. She will endure anything she must. And she will survive. Go girl power in this book, Leila rocks it! And just as Leila rocks it, Vlad is so intense and overbearing that it’s everything I’ve always known him to be! Oh, but if he was real I would stab him in his sleep. But this is top book boyfriend material, not just for now, but forever. Vlad has secured a permanent spot in my list of favorite heroes ever.<br><br>utc-top-pickThis book is not as hot as some might have expected after such infamous scenes that Ms. Frost has written. But every sex scene is so strategically placed and carries just the perfect emotion needed during that moment in the story! What a great job with that! And when I say not as hot, I don’t mean it’s dull. Vlad knows how to rock a girls world and he definitely does that and then some. Have I mentioned how much I need to change my name to Leila? Leila Dracula that is. <br><br>For the Night Huntress series fans out there, Cat is in this one! Beware that there is a huge spoiler if you haven’t read the last book in the Night Huntress series! But Cat gets the job done here as well. And some of our favorites from that series make a cameo in this one too, like Marie Laveau.<br><br>BOUND BY FLAMES is a pulse-pounding, electric and combustible ride! This series just gets better! This book is SAVAGE, that is probably the best way to describe it. I loved every single minute of it. If you’re not reading this now, you’re missing out. If you haven’t read this series yet, you’re missing out. I can’t wait for more!<br><br>Favorite quote:<br><br>“Months ago, you made me ask you if you would marry me. This time, I’m not asking. I’m telling you to say yes, so say it, and be mine for eternity.”<br>“Yes. Yesterday, today, forever… yes.”<br><br>*ARC provided by publisher</span>

    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1050546386?book_show_action=true">Sep 09, 2014</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Jennifer" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Jennifer" href="/user/show/4295616-jennifer">Jennifer</a>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1050546386" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer5569634265822185062"><strong>Originally posted at <a href='http://thebooknympho.com/2015/01/vlad-is-always-5-stars-bound-by-flames-by-jeaniene-frost/' target='_blank' rel='nofollow noopener'>The Book Nympho</a></strong><br/><br/><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1416919962i/12116748.png' alt='icon BOOKLOVE' width='100' height='100' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/>  <img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1422273861i/13479186.png' alt='icon fangtastic' width='100' height='100' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/>  <img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1422273861i/13479187.png' alt='Icon TOP READ' width='100' height='100' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/>  <img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1416827929i/12078248.png' alt='icon well written' width='100' height='100' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/>Just like the previous books in the Night Prince series, BOUND BY FLAMES is a 5 star read because Vlad never fails to rock my world!!<br/><br/>Vlad is just as savage as always when it comes to protecting the people he cares for and never more so than when Leila is in danger! While Vlad is awesome all on his own I've got to give Leila a huge shout out! She really came into her power and grew as a strong heroine in BOUND BY FLAMES.<br/><br/>Leila is still young in human years</span>
  <span id="freeText5569634265822185062" style="display:none"><strong>Originally posted at <a href="http://thebooknympho.com/2015/01/vlad-is-always-5-stars-bound-by-flames-by-jeaniene-frost/" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">The Book Nympho</a></strong><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1416919962i/12116748.png" alt="icon BOOKLOVE" width="100" height="100" class="gr-hostedUserImg">  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1422273861i/13479186.png" alt="icon fangtastic" width="100" height="100" class="gr-hostedUserImg">  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1422273861i/13479187.png" alt="Icon TOP READ" width="100" height="100" class="gr-hostedUserImg">  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1416827929i/12078248.png" alt="icon well written" width="100" height="100" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Just like the previous books in the Night Prince series, BOUND BY FLAMES is a 5 star read because Vlad never fails to rock my world!!<br><br>Vlad is just as savage as always when it comes to protecting the people he cares for and never more so than when Leila is in danger! While Vlad is awesome all on his own I've got to give Leila a huge shout out! She really came into her power and grew as a strong heroine in BOUND BY FLAMES.<br><br>Leila is still young in human years and just a baby to her new vampire life. She's quit and shy in some aspects and still second guesses herself and her worth to Vlad. She can't believe a man like Vlad has fallen in love with her. But as BOUND BY FLAMES processes, so does Leila's inner strength and she over comes some of her misgivings when it comes to herself worth.<br><br>Oh those pesky human relatives. LOL Leila's sister Gretchen drives everyone around her crazy, especially the vampires. I can't wait to see if she hooks up with one or becomes one. It would be like watching Cat's mom all over again. Perhaps she will be turned and later meet Ian...<br><br>Speaking of Cat... we get a short glimpse at Cat and Bones when Vlad reaches out for help. If you've not read <a href="http://thebooknympho.com/2014/02/review-up-from-the-grave-by-jeaniene-frost/" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">UP FROM THE GRAVE</a>, the last Night Huntress book you will want to read it BEFORE reading BOUND BY FLAMES or you'll get a spoiler when reading about Cat and Bones' cameo.<br><br>Cat and Bones are not the only Night Huntress World characters that show up. We also get to see Mencheres and a famous Ghoul Queen.<br><br>OMG the epilogue!! That was 5 stars all by itself. LOL I can't wait for Vlad and Leila's return in 2016!Frost fans will love BOUND BY FLAMES! If you have to met Vlad and Leila yet you should start with book 1, <a href="http://thebooknympho.com/2013/01/dual-review-once-burned-by-jeaniene-frost/" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">ONCE BURNED</a>.<br><br> <br> 
  <strong>Favorite Quote / Moment:</strong>
 <br><p>“<em>You aren’t just my weakness, Leila …You are my destruction.</em>"<br></p><p>The last ghouls I'd met had tried to eat me, and not in the romantic way.<br></p><p>"<em>Oh I prefer Leila Dracula,</em>" I said, grinning as I felt Vlad's foot trod down on mine.<br><br></p> 
  <strong> </strong>
 <br> 
  <strong>Sexual Content: Sex with mild details</strong>
 <br> <br><br> </span>

<div id="review_632932241" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/632932241" />
    <a title="Maja (The Nocturnal Library)" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/4551536-maja-the-nocturnal-library"><img alt="Maja (The Nocturnal Library)" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1350750103p2/4551536.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/632932241?book_show_action=true">Jun 04, 2013</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Maja (The Nocturnal Library)" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Maja (The Nocturnal Library)" href="/user/show/4551536-maja-the-nocturnal-library">Maja (The Nocturnal Library)</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/4551536-maja-the-nocturnal-library?shelf=failed-to-impress">failed-to-impress</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/4551536-maja-the-nocturnal-library?shelf=i-see-dead-people">i-see-dead-people</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/4551536-maja-the-nocturnal-library?shelf=paranormal-romance">paranormal-romance</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/4551536-maja-the-nocturnal-library?shelf=urban-fantasy">urban-fantasy</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/4551536-maja-the-nocturnal-library?shelf=reviewed-in-2015">reviewed-in-2015</a>
          </div>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer632932241" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer10042439269409027356">I love Alpha men as much as the next girl, truly I do. There’s just something about a man so utterly in control that hits all the right spots for me. And let’s admit it, among fictional Alpha guys, Vlad Tepes is the ultimate thrill. I mean, think about it – Vlad the Impaler… please note that I am trying so hard to ignore the pun potential and applaud my maturity… that Vlad, Dracul, a romantic hero! What’s not to like?<br/><br/>Apparently, quite a lot.<br/><br/>Frost’s formula worked for me at the beginning. I expec</span>
  <span id="freeText10042439269409027356" style="display:none">I love Alpha men as much as the next girl, truly I do. There’s just something about a man so utterly in control that hits all the right spots for me. And let’s admit it, among fictional Alpha guys, Vlad Tepes is the ultimate thrill. I mean, think about it – Vlad the Impaler… please note that I am trying so hard to ignore the pun potential and applaud my maturity… that Vlad, Dracul, a romantic hero! What’s not to like?<br><br>Apparently, quite a lot.<br><br>Frost’s formula worked for me at the beginning. I expected to enjoy having Vlad as a hero and enjoy it I did; until I started reading <i>Bound by Flames</i>, the third book in her ever-growing series. Here it became clear that even I have my limits because by chapter two, the whole my-way-or-the-highway business started getting on my last nerve. Oh, Frost tried to redeem Dracul later on, and she even succeeded to a certain degree, but the bitter taste of his early actions never really left my mouth.<br><br>For her part, Leila behaved quite admirably throughout. She refrained from rash decisions, she thought things through and she ended up winning every battle. But she rarely got there through conversation alone, and that told me all I needed to know about the couple.<br><br>Frost pushed her boundaries in this book, possibly even a bit too far for some reason. I wasn’t bothered by the action or the torture, only by the relationship dynamic. With only one book left, I’ll definitely be finishing Leila and Vlad’s story. I just hope the two will find some balance or I will be very disappointed.<br><br><a href="http://www.thenocturnallibrary.com" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380226536i/681142.png" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br></span>
  <a data-text-id="10042439269409027356" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>

<div class=" clearFloats bigBox"><div class="h2Container gradientHeaderContainer"><h2 class="brownBackground">Readers also enjoyed</h2></div><div class="bigBoxBody"><div class="bigBoxContent containerWithHeaderContent"><div class='bookCarousel'>
<div class='carouselRow' style='width: 3600px'>
<ul>
<li class='cover' id='bookCover_10518110'>
<a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/10518110-the-bite-before-christmas"><img alt="The Bite Before Christmas (Argeneau, #15.5; Night Huntress, #6.5)" src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/books/1328313295l/10518110._SX98_.jpg" />
</a>

  
<script type="text/javascript" charset="utf-8">
//<![CDATA[  

  function submitShelfLink(unique_id, book_id, shelf_id, shelf_name, submit_form, exclusive) {
    var checkbox_id = 'shelf_name_' + unique_id + '_' + shelf_id;
    var element = document.getElementById(checkbox_id)

    var checked = element.checked
    if (checked && exclusive) {
      // can't uncheck a radio by clicking it!
      return
    }
    if(document.getElementById("savingMessage")){
      Element.show('savingMessage')
    }
    var element_id = 'shelfInDropdownName_' + unique_id + '_' + shelf_id;
    Element.update(element_id, "saving...");
    if (submit_form) {
      Element.hide('shelfDropdown_' + unique_id)
      var form = document.getElementById('addBookForm' + book_id)
      if (form) {
        form.shelf.value = shelf_name
        form.onsubmit()
      }
    }
    else {
      var action = checked ? 'remove' : ''
      element.checked = !element.checked
      new Ajax.Request('/shelf/add_to_shelf', {asynchronous:true, evalScripts:true, onSuccess:function(request){shelfSubmitted(request, book_id, checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name)}, parameters:'book_id=' + book_id + '&name=' + shelf_name + '&a=' + action + '&authenticity_token=' + encodeURIComponent('d3BqEaNWDdA+7Q1BPtRU3m4FVpHI45c2ymZr1A1Dx1wUeoR/b8KJkQIHNT0Od4EzFdZQVsqLpGSgbLH9+SQkaA==')})
    }
  }

  function shelfSubmitted(request, book_id, checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name) {
    Element.update('shelfListfalse_' + book_id, request.responseText)
    afterShelfSave(checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name.escapeHTML())
  }

  function refreshGroupBox(group_id, book_id) {
    new Ajax.Updater('addGroupBooks' + book_id + '', '/group/add_book_box', {asynchronous:true, evalScripts:true, onSuccess:function(request){refreshGroupBoxComplete(request, book_id);}, parameters:'id=' + group_id + '&book_id=' + book_id + '&refresh=true' + '&authenticity_token=' + encodeURIComponent('6SGKkkWXinp31RPpmSWv1UyL7LazjjUm1Rc9Ja62uOaKK2T8iQMOO0s/K5Wphno4N1jqcbHmBnS/HecMWtFb0g==')})
  }
//]]>
</script>

<span id="freeTextContainer3575995694244417313">Jeaniene Frost is the New York Times, USA Today, and international bestselling author of the Night Huntress series, the Night Prince series, the Broken Destiny series, and the new Night Rebel series. To date, foreign rights for her novels have sold to twenty different countries. Jeaniene lives in Florida with her husband Matthew, who long ago accepted that she rarely cooks and always sleeps in on </span>
  <span id="freeText3575995694244417313" style="display:none">Jeaniene Frost is the New York Times, USA Today, and international bestselling author of the Night Huntress series, the Night Prince series, the Broken Destiny series, and the new Night Rebel series. To date, foreign rights for her novels have sold to twenty different countries. Jeaniene lives in Florida with her husband Matthew, who long ago accepted that she rarely cooks and always sleeps in on the weekends. Aside from writing, Jeaniene enjoys reading, poetry, watching movies with her husband, exploring old cemeteries, spelunking and traveling – by car. Airplanes, children, and cook books frighten her.<br /><br />For information on Jeaniene's books, book trailers, deleted scenes, creature mythology, and more, please visit: <a target="_blank" rel="noopener nofollow" href="http://www.jeanienefrost.com">www.jeanienefrost.com</a><br /></span>
